---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-                                                                                           -
-  This is the Tag Index Allocation List, please avoid modding used tags.                   -
-                                                                                           -
-  Used tags are listed under a mod name (ie, [FlatGrass]) or under the name "Reserved:".   -
-                                                                                           -
-  If "Reserved:" that means that those tags are reserved for the mod that they are under.  -
-                                                                                           -
-  Any tags under "Open Tags:" are free for use, mod authors should include a copy of this  -
-  file that includes updated tags that they plan to use, this keeps mods compatible.       -
-                                                                                           -
-  The Offset can be used for Allocation Fixups, however please note that the Offsets are   -
-  only accurate when you build your mod on clean un-modded 0.5.0.2 tags.                   -
-                                                                                           -
